<script src="https://www.bleague.jp/files/user/assets/js/jquery.colorbox.js?v=1513679619"></script>

<script>
$(".game_news").on('click', function(){
    gameNewsLink($(this).attr('data-team_media_id'), $(this).attr('data-game_date'))
});
// ツールチップBS
function tipsBoxscore() {
    var $tipsParent = $(document.querySelectorAll('.tips-parent > [data-tips]'));
    $tipsParent.off().on({
        'mouseenter': function(event) {
            var $tips = $('.bs-tips-wrap');
            if(!$tips.length) {
                $('body').append('<div class="bs-tips-wrap tips-wrap"><div class="tips-inner"><div class="tips-content"><span></span></div></div></div>');
                $tips = $('.bs-tips-wrap');
            }
            // 一度定義しないと取得値がおかしくなる
            var $this = $(this);
            var w = $this.outerWidth(true),
                h = $this.outerHeight(true),
                y = $this.offset().top,
                x = $this.offset().left,
                tipsW = $tips.width() / 2 - w / 2,
                tipsH = $tips.height(),
                txt = $this.data('tips');
            $tips.find('span').text(txt);
            $tips.css({
                top: y - tipsH,
                left: x - tipsW
            });
            var w = $this.outerWidth(true),
                h = $this.outerHeight(true),
                y = $this.offset().top,
                x = $this.offset().left,
                tipsW = $tips.width() / 2 - w / 2,
                tipsH = $tips.height(),
                txt = $this.data('tips');
            $tips.find('span').text(txt);
            $tips.css({
                top: y - tipsH,
                left: x - tipsW
            }).show();
        },
        'mouseleave': function(event) {
            $('.bs-tips-wrap').hide();
        }
    });
}
//スコアをクリックしたとき
$(document).on('click', '#game__result .tab_wrap ul.first_tab > li', function() {
    // 遅延処理
    setTimeout(tipsBoxscore, 1000);
});
</script>
